msg);\n}, null);\n\n//MQTT publish\nGPIO.set_button_handler(pin, GPIO.PULL_UP, GPIO.INT_EDGE_NEG, 200, function() {\n  let res = MQTT.pub(topic, JSON.stringify({ bell: 1}), 1);\n  print('Published:', res ?
